<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ладить.html>ла́дить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">láditʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сладить.html>сла́дить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sláditʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сла́живать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make, to produce</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to arrange, to manage, to settle</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">perfective only<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to overcome, to defeat</li>

***сладкий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сладкий.html>сла́дкий</a> (2309)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">сладъкъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sladŭkŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*soldъkъ</i>. See also the dialectal Russian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">соло́дкий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">solódkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a doublet.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сладкий.html>сла́дкий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sládkij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)сла́ще</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сладча́йший</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sweet (having a pleasant taste)</li>
<li>sugary</li></ol>

<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="выступает в роли существительного">субстантивир.</span>, <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="разговорное">разг.</span> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:употребляться.html>употребля́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ласковый.html>ла́сковое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обращение.html>обраще́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тому</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кого́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>любим</a></i> <span class="example-fullblock"><br><span class="example-block" style="color:darkgreen">― <a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>Вот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мой</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:сладкий.html>сла́дкий</a></span>, ― Клаудиа <a href = vnd.unilang:снова.html>сно́ва</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:загадочный.html>загадочно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:улыбнуться.html>улыбну́лась</a>, ― <a href = vnd.unilang:поехать.html>пое́хали</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отсюда.html>отсю́да</a>. <span class="example-details" style="font-size:smaller;"> <i>Николай Желунов, «Рагомор», <span class="example-date">2007</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>г</a>.<span class="citation-source"> <span class="nkrja-source" style="font-size: x-small; font-style: italic;"></span></span></i></span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:слазить.html>сла́зить</a> (21635)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слазить.html>сла́зить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slázitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слезть.html>слезть</a></b>)

<ol><li>to climb down</li></ol>

***сласть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сласть.html>сласть</a> (28317)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu"><a href = vnd.unilang:сласть.html>сласть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slastĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*solstь</i>. The native <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">*солость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*solostĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is unattested, but is the source of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">солости́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">solostítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сласть.html>сласть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slastʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сласть.html>сла́сти</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сласть.html>сла́сти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сласть.html>сласте́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> rare</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sweetness</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pleasure, enjoyment, candies</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">plural only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sweets</li></ol>

***слать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:слать.html>слать</a> (754)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">сълати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sŭlati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sъlati</i>, from either <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*selh₁-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">favourable</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*selh₂-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mercy, comfort</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слать.html>слать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:послать.html>посла́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to send, to dispatch
<ul><li><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white">Александр Солженицын, <i>Матренин <a href = vnd.unilang:двор.html>двор</a></i> 1968:<dl><dd><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:перечислять.html>перечисля́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>други́х</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйка.html>хозя́ек</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кого́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бу́дет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> поко́йней <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> угожей, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:слать.html>сла́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:обойти.html>обойти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>их</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oná perečisljála mne drugíx xozjájek, u kovó búdet mne pokójnej i ugožej, i <b>slála</b> obojtí ix</i></dd><dd>she listed me other (home)owners with whom I could be more comfortable and at ease and she <b>sent</b> me to visit them</dd></dl></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:слащавый.html>слаща́вый</a> (30060)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слащавый.html>слаща́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slaščávyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)слаща́вее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)слаща́вей</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>mushy; sickly; sugary; schmaltzy</li></ol>

***слегка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:слегка.html>слегка́</a> (953)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слегка.html>слегка́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slexká</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>lightly, slightly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:слегка.html>слегка́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ранний.html>ра́нен</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>slexká</b> ránen.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I <b>slightly</b> hurt myself.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>in passing</li>
<li>easily</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***след.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:след.html>след</a> (573)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">слѣдъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slědŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:след.html>след</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sled</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:след.html>сле́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:след.html>следы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:след.html>следо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>track
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустить.html>пусти́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ложный.html>ло́жному</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:след.html>сле́ду</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pustítʹ po lóžnomu <b>slédu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to throw off <b>the trail</b>, misguide</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>footprint, footstep</li>
<li>trace, sign</li>
<li>vestige</li>
<li>print</li>
<li>sole of a sock or stocking</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:след.html>след</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sled</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:следить.html>следи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sledítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проследить.html>проследи́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">отследи́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выследить.html>вы́следить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to watch, to follow, to spy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:следить.html>следи́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>языко́м</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Sledí</b> za jazykóm!</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Watch</b> (your) tongue! (informal)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to look after <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. health</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to keep an eye on</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li>to leave traces or footprints behind</li></ol>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:следование.html>сле́дование</a> (14307)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:следовать.html>сле́довать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slédovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ание</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-anije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:следование.html>сле́дование</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slédovanije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:следование.html>сле́дования</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:следование.html>сле́дования</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:следование.html>сле́дований</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>movement
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поезд.html>по́езд</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дальний.html>да́льнего</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:следование.html>сле́дования</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pójezd dálʹnevo <b>slédovanija</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">long-distance train</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всём</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>пути́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:следование.html>сле́дования</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na vsjóm putí <b>slédovanija</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">throughout the entire journey</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>пути́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:следование.html>сле́дования</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:войско.html>во́йск</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">po putí <b>slédovanija</b> vójsk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">along/on the line of march</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:маршрут.html>маршру́т</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:следование.html>сле́дования</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">maršrút <b>slédovanija</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">route</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>compliance
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:следование.html>сле́дование</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:закон.html>зако́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>slédovanije</b> zakónu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">compliance with the law</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:следование.html>сле́дование</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:предписание.html>предписа́ниям</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:врач.html>врача́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>slédovanije</b> predpisánijam vračá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">compliance with the doctor's recommendations</span></div></dd>

***следовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:следовать.html>сле́довать</a> (372)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:след.html>след</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sled</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:следовать.html>сле́довать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slédovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:последовать.html>после́довать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to follow, to go after</li>
<li>to follow, to be next</li>
<li>to follow, to take after</li>
<li>to follow, to do accordingly</li>
<li>to be bound to <i>(a port)</i></li>
<li>to follow, to be a consequence</li>
<li>to should, to ought to (<i>the agent who/which should/ought to do something is in the dative case</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:следовать.html>сле́дует</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:срочно.html>сро́чно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прибыть.html>прибы́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вокзал.html>вокза́л</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jemú <b>slédujet</b> sróčno pribýtʹ na vokzál.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He <b>should</b> urgently arrive at the station.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b>сле́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать</b>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">сльза</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slĭza</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*slьza</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слеза.html>слеза́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slezá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слеза.html>слезы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слеза.html>слёзы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слеза.html>слёз</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слезть.html>слезть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sleztʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слезать.html>слеза́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slezátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слезть.html>слезть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to come down, to get down <i>(from)</i>, to dismount <i>(from)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come down</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(from a train, bus etc)</i> to get out <i>(of)</i>, to get off</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to peel off, to come off</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слеза.html>слеза́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slezá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ли́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слезливый.html>слезли́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">slezlívyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)слезли́вее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)слезли́вей</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>given to crying; schmaltzy; tearful, lachrymose</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:слеза.html>слез</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:выя.html>вы́й</a></b>
